        +String apiVersion
        +String kind
        +Object metadata

        +Resources resources
        +Array startupTaints
        +Array taints
    }
    class Kubelet {
        +Array clusterDNS
        +Boolean cpuCFSQuota
        +Object evictionHard
        +Integer evictionMaxPodGracePeriod
        +Object evictionSoft
        +Object evictionSoftGracePeriod
        +Integer imageGCHighThresholdPercent
        +Integer imageGCLowThresholdPercent
        +Object kubeReserved
        +Integer maxPods
        +Integer podsPerCore
        +Object systemReserved
    }
    class NodeClassRef {
        +String apiVersion
        +String kind
        +String name
    }
    class Resources {
        +Object requests
    }
    class Requirement {
        +String key
        +Integer minValues
        +String operator
        +Array values
    }
    class Taint {
        +String effect
        +String key
        +String timeAdded
        +String value
    }
    class NodeClaimStatus {
        +Object allocatable
        +Object capacity
        +Array conditions
        +String imageID
        +String nodeName
        +String providerID
    }
    class Condition {
        +String lastTransitionTime
        +String message
        +String reason
        +String severity
        +String status
        +String type
    }

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Created
    Created --> Pending: NodeClaim Created
    Pending --> Initializing: Node Provisioned
    Initializing --> Ready: Node Initialized
    Ready --> Terminating: Delete Requested
    Pending --> Failed: Provisioning Failed
    Initializing --> Failed: Initialization Failed
    Terminating --> [*]
    Failed --> [*]
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
graph TD
    A[NodeClaim] --> B[spec]
    A --> C[status]
    B --> D[nodeClassRef]
    B --> E[requirements]
    B --> F[kubelet]
    B --> G[resources]
    B --> H[taints]
    B --> I[startupTaints]
    F --> J[evictionHard]
    F --> K[evictionSoft]
    F --> L[kubeReserved]
    F --> M[systemReserved]
    F --> N[clusterDNS]
    C --> O[nodeName]
    C --> P[providerID]
    C --> Q[capacity]
    C --> R[allocatable]
    C --> S[conditions]
    D --> T[Provider Config]
    E --> U[Instance Type]
    E --> V[Zone]
    E --> W[Capacity Type]
```
